Action.c(37):     **\n

Action.c(37):     **\n

Action.c(37):     **       HTML form element; make it the same as the object name\n

Action.c(37):     **       doesn't support the type property for for elements)\n
Action.c(37):     **     text\n
Action.c(37):     **     textarea\n

Action.c(37):     **     select\n
Action.c(37):     **\n
Action.c(37):     **   uptoSnuff: function call that's evaluated during validation check\n

Action.c(37):     **     isRadio(formObj)\n

Action.c(37):       this.eltType = eltType;\n
Action.c(37):       this.upToSnuff = upToSnuff;\n

Action.c(37):     \n
Action.c(37):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(37):     ** create a new object for each form element you need to validate\n

Action.c(37):     xx-xxx-xxxx');\n

Action.c(37):     **   isText(str): verifies text input or textarea is not empty\n

Action.c(37):     **   isRadio(formObj): verifies one of a group of radio buttons is chosen\n
Action.c(37):     **   isCheck(formObj, form, [begin], [num]): verifies at least one\n
Action.c(37):     **       of a group of checkboxes is checked\n
Action.c(37):     **     for [begin], fill in the index number in the elements array\n
Action.c(37):     **         of the first checkbox (remember to start counting from zero)\n
Action.c(37):     **     for [num], fill in the number of checkboxes in the group\n
Action.c(37):     **\n
Action.c(37):     ** validate text in text input or textarea matches pattern\n
Action.c(37):     **   isEmail(str): verifies email address (contains "@" and ".")\n
Action.c(37):     **   isState(str): verifies U.S. State Code\n
Action.c(37):     **   isZipCode(str): verifies zip code of form xxxxx or xxxxx-xxxx\n
Action.c(37):     **   isPhoneNum(str): verifies phone number of form xxx-xxx-xxxx\n
Action.c(37):     **   isDate(str): verifies date of form mm/dd/yyyy\n
Action.c(37):     ***************************************************************/\n
Action.c(37):     \n
Action.c(37):     function isText(str) {\n
Action.c(37):       return (str != "");\n
Action.c(37):     }\n
Action.c(37):     \n
Action.c(37):     function isSelect(formObj) {\n
Action.c(37):       return (formObj.selectedIndex != 0);\n
Action.c(37):     }\n
Action.c(37):     \n
Action.c(37):     function isRadio(formObj) {\n
Action.c(37):       for (j=0; j<formObj.length; j++) {\n
Action.c(37):         if (formObj[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(37):           return true;\n
Action.c(37):         }\n
Action.c(37):       }\n
Action.c(37):       return false;\n
Action.c(37):     }\n
Action.c(37):     \n
Action.c(37):     function isCheck(formObj, form, begin, num) {\n
Action.c(37):       for (j=begin; j<begin+num; j++) {\n
Action.c(37):         if (form.elements[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(37):           return true;\n
Action.c(37):         }\n
Action.c(37):       }\n
Action.c(37):       return false;\n
Action.c(37):     }\n
Action.c(37):     \n
Action.c(37):     function isEmail(str) {\n
Action.c(37):       return ((str != "") && (str.indexOf("@") != -1) && (str.indexOf(".") != -1));\n
Action.c(37):     }\n
Action.c(37):     \n

Action.c(37):     ** define and instantiate validation objects\n
Action.c(37):     ** the validation object accepts the following parameters:\n
Action.c(37):     **\n
Action.c(37):     **   realName: name used in the alerts (same as label on the page)\n
Action.c(37):     **\n
Action.c(37):     **   formEltName: this must be the name of the corresponding\n
Action.c(37):     **       HTML form element; make it the same as the object name\n
Action.c(37):     **\n
Action.c(37):     **   eltType: element type (we have to create this since IE3\n
Action.c(37):     **       doesn't support the type property for for elements)\n
Action.c(37):     **     text\n
Action.c(37):     **     textarea\n
Action.c(37):     **     checkbox\n
Action.c(37):     **     radio\n
Action.c(37):     **     select\n
Action.c(37):     **\n
Action.c(37):     **   uptoSnuff: function call that's evaluated during validation check\n
Action.c(37):     **     isText(str)\n
Action.c(37):     **     isSelect(formObj)\n
Action.c(37):     **     isRadio(formObj)\n
Action.c(37):     **     isCheck(formObj, form, [index of first checkbox in group],\n
Action.c(37):     **         [number of checkboxes])\n
Action.c(37):     **     isEmail(str)\n
Action.c(37):     **     isState(str)\n
Action.c(37):     **     isZipCode(str)\n
Action.c(37):     **     isPhoneNum(str)\n
Action.c(37):     **     isDate(str)\n
Action.c(37):     **\n
Action.c(37):     **   format: text representation of required format;\n
Action.c(37):     **       pass 'null' if no required format;\n

Action.c(37):     ***************************************************************/\n
Action.c(37):     \n

Action.c(37):     function validation(realName, formEltName, eltType, upToSnuff, format) {\n

Action.c(37):       this.formEltName = formEltName;\n
Action.c(37):       this.eltType = eltType;\n
Action.c(37):       this.upToSnuff = upToSnuff;\n
Action.c(37):       this.format = format;\n
Action.c(37):     }\n
Action.c(37):     \n
Action.c(37):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(37):     ** create a new object for each form element you need to validate\n
